    <script type="text/javascript">
        var Linguaggio;
        var urlFile = "";
        var UploadFileTitle = "";
        var UploadFileName = "";
        var UploadFileType = "";

        var localMode = false;
        var info;

        var indiceFinestra = 1;

        function openReport(idScenario) {
            var urlReport = (!localMode) ? "/makereport.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/makereport.ashx";
            urlReport += "?idscenario=" + idScenario ;
            this.location=urlReport;

        }


        function showAttendere(messaggio) {
            if (messaggio === undefined)
                $('#TextLoading')[0].innerHTML = "";
            else
                $('#TextLoading')[0].innerHTML = messaggio;
            $('#Loading').show();
           
        }
        function hideAttendere() {
            $('#Loading').hide();
           
        }
        

        function openDettaglio(idScenario) {


            var scenario = $("#gridScenari").jqxGrid("source").records.find(x => x.IDSCENARIO == idScenario);
            var value = scenario.CDESCRIZIONE.replace(info.CurrentDirectory, "").replace("\\Scenari\\", "").replace(".ibt", "")


            $(document.body).append('<div  id="newWindow' + indiceFinestra + '"><div style="background-color: aliceblue;font-weight: bolder;">' + value + " ( " +
                scenario.DINIZIO.toLocaleDateString() + " " + scenario.DINIZIO.toLocaleTimeString() + " )"
                + '</div><div id = "Content' + indiceFinestra + '"><div id="gridDettaglio_' + indiceFinestra + '"</div></div>');

            $('#newWindow' + indiceFinestra).jqxWindow({ height: 580, width: 1100, position: { x: 50, y: 200 } });



            var urlCasoScenario = (!localMode) ? "/serializetable.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/serializetable.ashx";
            urlCasoScenario += "?query=select * from ABCASOSCENARIO where IDSCENARIO='" + idScenario + "' order by riga ";

            var sourceCasoScenario =
            {
                datatype: "json",
                datafields: [
                    { name: 'IDCASOSCENARIO', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'IDSCENARIO', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'DINIZIO', type: 'date' },
                    { name: 'DFINIE', type: 'date' },
                    { name: 'CESITO', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'CSTATO', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'INPUT', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'RECORD', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'VARIABILI', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'LOG', type: 'string' },
                    { name: 'RIGA', type: 'int' },
                ],
                id: 'IDCASOSCENARIO',
                url: urlCasoScenario,
                root: 'data',
                editmode: 'selectedcell'
            };
            var dataAdapterCasoScenario = new $.jqx.dataAdapter(sourceCasoScenario, {
                downloadComplete: function (data, status, xhr) { },
                loadComplete: function (data) { },
                loadError: function (xhr, status, error) { }
            });


            $("#gridDettaglio_" + indiceFinestra).jqxGrid(
                {
                    width: "99%",
                    source: dataAdapterCasoScenario,
                    localization: getLocalization('it'),

                    columnsresize: true,
                    columnsreorder: true,
                    filterable: true,
                    autoshowfiltericon: true,

                    pageable: true,
                    pagesize: 10,
                    pagesizeoptions: ['5', '10', '15', '20', '25', '30', '40', '50'],

                    autoheight: true,
                    sortable: true,
                    autoheight: true,
                    autorowheight: true,
                    sortable: true,
                    sortmode: 'many',

                    altrows: true,
                    enabletooltips: true,
                    editable: false,
                    selectionmode: 'none',

                    columns: [

                        { text: 'Riga', datafield: 'RIGA', align: 'right', cellsalign: 'right', width: 70 },

                        {
                            text: 'Data inizio', datafield: 'DINIZIO', width: 150, columntype: 'datetimeinput',
                            filtertype: 'date', width: 200, cellsformat: 'dd-MMMM-yyyy HH:mm:ss'
                        },
                        {
                            text: 'Data fine', datafield: 'DFINIE', width: 150, columntype: 'datetimeinput',
                            filtertype: 'date', width: 200, cellsformat: 'dd-MMMM-yyyy HH:mm:ss'
                        },
                        { text: 'Esito', datafield: 'CESITO', width: 300, filtertype: 'checkedlist', cellsrenderer: colonnaEsito },
                        { text: 'Input', datafield: 'INPUT', width: 70, filtertype: 'none', cellsrenderer: colonnaInput },
                        { text: 'Variabili', datafield: 'VARIABILI', width: 70, filtertype: 'none', cellsrenderer: colonnaVariabili },
                        { text: 'Record', datafield: 'RECORD', width: 70, filtertype: 'none', cellsrenderer: colonnaRecord },
                        { text: 'LOG', datafield: 'LOG', width: 70, filtertype: 'none', cellsrenderer: colonnaLog },

                    ]

                });












            indiceFinestra++;

            // alert(idScenario);
        }


        var arrayInput = [];
        function openInput(riga, idgrid) {

            $(document.body).append('<div  id="newWindow' +
                indiceFinestra +
                '"><div style="background-color: cornflowerblue;font-weight: bolder;">Input</div>' +
                '<div id="Content' + indiceFinestra + '"><div style="overflow-y: scroll;" id="jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra + '"</div></div>');
            $('#newWindow' + indiceFinestra).jqxWindow({ height: 700, width: 600, position: { x: 50, y: 50 } });


            var record = $("#" + idgrid).jqxGrid("source").records[riga];
            var input = JSON.parse(record.INPUT);
            /* formato input
             * [
             *    Titolo
             *    Values[]
             *          Value Label Tipo (variabililocali o input)
             * ]
             */
            var source = [];
            input.forEach(function (item) {
                var maschera = {};
                maschera.label = item.Titolo;
                maschera.icon = "/images/icons8-form-24_1.png";
                var sourceItems = [];
                item.Values.forEach(function (valori) {
                    var dato = {}
                    dato.label = valori.Label + " = " + valori.Value;
                    dato.icon = (valori.Tipo === 'variabililocali') ? "/images/icons8-variabile-24.png" : "/images/icons8-modulo-di-input-di-testo-24.png";
                    sourceItems.push(dato);
                });
                maschera.items = sourceItems;
                source.push(maschera);
            });
            $('#jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra).jqxTree({ source: source, width: '99%', height: '99%' });
            indiceFinestra++;
        }

        function openVariabili(riga, idgrid) {

            $(document.body).append('<div  id="newWindow' +
                indiceFinestra +
                '"><div style="background-color: cornflowerblue;font-weight: bolder;">Variabili</div>' +
                '<div id="Content' + indiceFinestra + '"><div style="overflow-y: scroll;" id="jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra + '"</div></div>');
            $('#newWindow' + indiceFinestra).jqxWindow({ height: 700, width: 600, position: { x: 50, y: 50 } });


            var record = $("#" + idgrid).jqxGrid("source").records[riga];
            var input = JSON.parse(record.VARIABILI);
            /* formato input
             * [
             *   name
             *   value
             * ]
             */
            var source = [];
            input.forEach(function (item) {

                var maschera = {};
                maschera.label = item.name + " = " + item.value;
                maschera.icon = "/images/icons8-variabile-24.png";
                source.push(maschera);
            });
            $('#jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra).jqxTree({ source: source, width: '99%', height: '99%' });
            indiceFinestra++;
        }


        function openRecord(riga, idgrid) {
            $(document.body).append('<div  id="newWindow' +
                indiceFinestra +
                '"><div style="background-color: cornflowerblue;font-weight: bolder;">Record</div>' +
                '<div id="Content' + indiceFinestra + '"><div style="overflow-y: scroll;" id="jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra + '"</div></div>');
            $('#newWindow' + indiceFinestra).jqxWindow({ height: 700, width: 600, position: { x: 50, y: 50 } });


            var record = $("#" + idgrid).jqxGrid("source").records[riga];
            var input = JSON.parse(record.RECORD);
            /* formato input
             * [
             *   name
             *   value
             * ]
             */
            var source = [];
            Object.getOwnPropertyNames(input).forEach(function (item) {
                var maschera = {};
                maschera.label = item + " = " + input[item];
                maschera.icon = "/images/icons8-variabile-24.png";
                source.push(maschera);
            })
            $('#jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra).jqxTree({ source: source, width: '99%', height: '99%' });
            indiceFinestra++;
        }

        function agganciaAzione(item) {
            var maschera = {};
            maschera.label = item.descrizione;
            var sourceItems = [];

            if (item.messaggio != null) {
                var o = {};
                o.label = item.messaggio;
                o.icon = "/images/icons8-info-24.png";
                sourceItems.push(o);
            }



            if (item.esito)
                maschera.icon = "/images/icons8-casella-di-controllo-selezionata-24.png";
            else
                maschera.icon = "/images/icons8-fail-24.png";

            if (Array.isArray(item.azioni)) {

                item.azioni.forEach(function (questo) {
                    sourceItems.push(agganciaAzione(questo));
                });

            }
            if (sourceItems.length > 0)
                maschera.items = sourceItems;

            return maschera;

        }
        function openLog(riga, idgrid) {

            $(document.body).append('<div  id="newWindow' +
                indiceFinestra +
                '"><div style="background-color: cornflowerblue;font-weight: bolder;">Log</div>' +
                '<div id="Content' + indiceFinestra + '"><div style="overflow-y: scroll;" id="jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra + '"</div></div>');
            $('#newWindow' + indiceFinestra).jqxWindow({ height: 700, width: 800, position: { x: 50, y: 50 } });


            var record = $("#" + idgrid).jqxGrid("source").records[riga];
            var input = JSON.parse(record.LOG);
            /* formato input
             * [
             *    descrizione
             *    messaggio
             *    esito
             *    azioni
             * ]
             * oppure potrebbe partire con
             *   nodo
             *   e azioni
             */

            if (!Array.isArray(input))
                input = input.azioni;
            var source = [];
            input.forEach(function (item) {
                source.push(agganciaAzione(item));
                /*
                var sourceItems = [];
                item.Values.forEach(function (valori) {
                    var dato = {}
                    dato.label = valori.Label + " = " + valori.Value;
                    dato.icon = (valori.Tipo==='variabililocali')?"/images/icons8-variabile-24.png":"/images/icons8-modulo-di-input-di-testo-24.png";
                    sourceItems.push(dato);
                });
                maschera.items = sourceItems;
                */
                // source.push(maschera);
            });
            $('#jqxTree_' + indiceFinestra).jqxTree({ source: source, width: '99%', height: '99%' });
            indiceFinestra++;
        }



        var colonnaTesto = function (row, column, value) {

            if (value.length > 100)
                value = value.substring(0, 97) + "..."

            return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;">' + value + "</div>";
        }
        var colonnaNomeScenario = function (row, column, value) {

            value = value.replace(info.CurrentDirectory, "");
            value = value.replace("\\Scenari\\", "");
            value = value.replace(".ibt", "");
            if (value.length > 100)
                value = value.substring(0, 97) + "..."

            return '<div    class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;font-size:12px">' + value + "</div>";
        }
        var colonnaStato = function (row, column, value) {

            if (value == 'Terminato')
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;">' + value + "</div>";
            else
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;background-color: burlywood;">' + value + "</div>";
        }

        var colonnaEsito = function (row, column, value) {

            if (value == 'SUCCESS')
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;background-color: green;color:white">' + value + "</div>";
            else
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-left-align" style="margin-top: 4px;background-color: red;color:white">' + value + "</div>";
        }

        var colonnaFailed = function (row, column, value) {

            if (value == '0' || value == undefined || value == '')
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-right-align" style="margin-top: 4px;">' + value + "</div>";
            else
                return '<div class="jqx-grid-cell-right-align" style="margin-top: 4px;color: red;">' + value + "</div>";
        }

        var colonnaDettagli = function (row, column, value) {
            return "<img onclick='openDettaglio(\"" + value + "\")' src='images/icons8-pannello-dettagli-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>" +
                "&nbsp;<img  title ='Elimina' onclick='deleteReport(\"" + value + "\")' src='images/icons8-elimina-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>" +
                "&nbsp;<img onclick='openReport(\"" + value + "\")' src='images/icons8-ms-excel-report-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>";
        }

      

        var colonnaInput = function (row, column, value) {
            if (value.length == 0)
                return "";
            return "<img onclick='openInput(" + row + ",     \"" + this.element.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.id + "\")' src='images/icons8-ingressi-multipli-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>";
        }
        var colonnaVariabili = function (row, column, value) {
            if (value.length == 0)
                return "";
            return "<img onclick='openVariabili(" + row + ",     \"" + this.element.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.id + "\")' src='images/icons8-variabile-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>";
        }
        var colonnaRecord = function (row, column, value) {
            if (value.length == 0)
                return "";
            return "<img onclick='openRecord(" + row + ",     \"" + this.element.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.id + "\")' src='images/icons8-banca-dati-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>";
        }
        var colonnaLog = function (row, column, value) {
            if (value.length == 0)
                return "";
            return "<img onclick='openLog(" + row + ",     \"" + this.element.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.id + "\")' src='images/icons8-log-36.png' style='margin-left: 5px;cursor:pointer'>";
        }
        $(document).ready(function () {


            /*
             * impostazione pannello workspace
            */
            $('#workspaces').jqxDropDownButton({ arrowSize: 0, height: 50, dropDownWidth: 300, width: 300 });
            $('#workspaces').jqxDropDownButton('setContent', '<span style="position: relative; line-height: 52px; margin-left: 3px; margin-top: 5px;">' +
                '<img src="images/icons8-workspace-48.png" style="vertical-align: middle;padding-right: 10px"><span id="wsname" class="titolo" ></span ></span > ');



            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: (!localMode) ? "/info.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/info.ashx",
                cache: false,
                dataType: "json",
                async: true,
                success: function (data) {
                    info = data;
                    $("#titolo").text(data.Titolo);
                    $("#servizio").text(data.Servizio);
                   //$("#workingdir").text(data.WorkingDir);
                   $("#versione").text(data.Linguaggio.Versione + ": " + data.Versione);
                 
                    $("#wsname").text(data.Workspace);
                    $("#informazioni").text("Working dir = "+data.WorkingDir+" Unique ID = "+data.uniqueID);
                    Linguaggio = data.Linguaggio;

                    var source = [];
                    data.workspaces.forEach(function (item) {

                        source.push({
                            label: item,
                            selected: item == data.Workspace,
                            icon: "images/icons8-workspace-32.png"
                        })
                    });

                    $('#Application').jqxTree({ source: source, width: '100%', height: '100%' });
                    $('#Application').on('select', function (event) {
                        var args = event.args;
                        var item = $('#Application').jqxTree('getItem', args.element);
                        $("#wsname").text(item.label);
                        $('#workspaces').jqxDropDownButton('close');
                        //   var url=(!localMode) ? "/setworkspace.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/setworkspace.ashx"
                        var url = (!localMode) ? "/changeworkspace.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/changeworkspace.ashx"

                        $.ajax({
                            type: "GET",
                            url: url + "?titolo=" + item.label,
                            cache: false,
                            dataType: "json",
                            async: true,
                            success: function (data) {
                                location.reload();

                            },
                            error: function (err) {

                                alert("Error ");

                            }
                        });


                    });

                },
                error: function (err) {
                    /*
                    if (notifica != null) {
                        $("#notificagetDataTable").jqxNotification("close");
                        $("#notificagetDataTable").remove();
                    }
                    */


                }
            });


            $('#Browsers').jqxDropDownButton({ arrowSize: 0, height: 50, dropDownWidth: 350, width: 350 });
            $('#Browsers').jqxDropDownButton('setContent', '<span style="position: relative; line-height: 52px; margin-left: 3px; margin-top: 5px;">' +
                '<img id="browserimage" src="images/icons8-hourglass-done-48.png" style="vertical-align: middle;padding-right: 10px"><span id="browsername" class="titoloPiccolo" ></span ></span > ');

            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "/listabrowser.ashx" ,
                cache: false,
                dataType: "json",
                async: true,
                success: function (data) {
                   
                

                    var source = [];
                    data.forEach(function (item) {
                        if (item.presente) {
                            
                            switch (item.chiave) {
                                case "Chrome":
                                case "Chrome Beta":
                                case "Chrome Dev":
                                case "Chrome Canary":
                                    immagine = "images/icons8-chrome-32.png";
                                    break;
                                case "Edge":
                                case "Edge Beta":
                                case "Edge Dev":
                                case "Edge Canary":
                                    immagine = "images/icons8-microsoft-edge-32.png";

                                    break;

                                    immagine = "images/icons8-internet-explorer-32.png";
                                    break;


                            }
                            source.push({
                                label: item.descrizione + " " + item.versione,
                                chiave: item.chiave,
                                //selected: item == data.Workspace,
                                icon: immagine
                            })
                        }
                    });

                    $('#Browser').jqxTree({ source: source, width: '100%', height: '100%' });
                    $('#Browser').on('select', function (event) {
                        var args = event.args;
                        var item = $('#Browser').jqxTree('getItem', args.element);
                        $('#Browsers').jqxDropDownButton('close');
                        $("#browsername").text(item.label);
                        $("#browserimage").attr('src', item.icon.replace("32", "48"));
                       
                    });

                },
                error: function (err) {
                    /*
                    if (notifica != null) {
                        $("#notificagetDataTable").jqxNotification("close");

                    }
                    */

        function downloadGridReport() {
            
            var righe = $("#gridScenari").jqxGrid('getrows');
            for ( i = 0; i < righe.length; i++)
                 righe[i].CJSON = '';
            var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
            
            request.open('POST', "/gridexcel.ashx", true);
            request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8');
            request.responseType = 'blob';
           

            request.onload = function (e) {
                hideAttendere();
                if (this.status === 200) {
                    var fileName = "I_ABAT.xlsx";
                   
                    var blob = this.response;
                    if (window.navigator.msSaveOrOpenBlob) {
                        window.navigator.msSaveBlob(blob, fileName);
                    }
                    else {
                        var downloadLink = window.document.createElement('a');
                        var contentTypeHeader = request.getResponseHeader("Content-Type");
                        downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([blob], { type: contentTypeHeader }));
                        downloadLink.download = fileName;
                        document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                        downloadLink.click();
                        document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                    }
                }
            };
            showAttendere("Preparazione file Excel");
            request.send("Records=" + encodeURI(JSON.stringify(righe).replaceAll('&','ยง')));
            /*
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                data: {
                    Records: JSON.stringify(righe)
                   
                },
              
                url: "/gridexcel.ashx",
                cache: false,
                dataType: "json",
                async: true,
                success: function (data) {
                     if (data.errore != '') {
                        $('#erroriinnerPopup').html(data.errore);
                        $('#errori').jqxWindow('open');
                    }
                },
                error: function (err) {
                    $('#erroriinnerPopup').html(err.responseText);
                    $('#errori').jqxWindow('open');
                }
            });
            */
        }
        function deleteReport(idScenario) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "/deletescenario.ashx?idscenario=" + idScenario,
                cache: false,
                dataType: "json",
                async: true,
                success: function (data) {
                    $('#progress').hide();
                    if (!data.ok != '') {

                        $('#erroriinnerPopup').html(data.errore);
                        $('#errori').jqxWindow('open');
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#gridScenari").jqxGrid('updatebounddata');

                    }
                },
                error: function (err) {

                    $('#erroriinnerPopup').html(err.responseText);
                    $('#errori').jqxWindow('open');
                }
            });
        }
        function clickMenu(sender, Operazione, Tag, Testo) {
            switch (Operazione) {
                case "OpenReport":

                    $('#viewRpt')[0].src = "report.html?file=" + Tag + "&guid=" + createGuid();
                    $('#TitleDialogFile').text("'" + Testo + "'  " + Linguaggio.ElencoReport);
                    $('#rpt').jqxWindow('open');
                    //  $('#rpt').css("z-index", "9999");
                    break;
                case "EseguiScenario":
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        
                        $("#jqxMenu").jqxMenu('close');
                    }, 100);
                  $('#viewRpt')[0].src = "esegui.html?file=" + Tag + "&browser=" + $("#browsername").text()+"&guid=" + createGuid();
                    $('#TitleDialogFile').text("Esegui Scenario " + Testo);
                    $('#rpt').jqxWindow('open');
                    break;
                case "EseguiProcesso":
                    setTimeout(function () {

                        $("#jqxMenu").jqxMenu('close');
                    }, 100);
                    $("#jqxMenu").jqxMenu('close')
                    $('#viewRpt')[0].src = "eseguiProcesso.html?file=" + Tag + "&guid=" + createGuid();
                    $('#TitleDialogFile').text("Esegui Processo " + Testo);
                    $('#rpt').jqxWindow('open');
                    //  $('#rpt').css("z-index", "9999");
                    break;
                case "UploadDati":
                    url: (!localMode) ? "/UploadDati.ashx" : "http://127.0.0.1:8201/UploadDati.ashx",
                        $('#errori').jqxWindow('close');

                    var divpadre = $(sender).parent().parent().parent().parent();
                    var ul = $(sender).parent().parent().parent();
                    var li = $(sender).parent().parent();

                    if ($(divpadre).attr('altezza') === undefined) {
                        $(divpadre)[0].setAttribute('altezza', $(divpadre).height())
                        $(ul)[0].setAttribute('altezza', $(ul).height())
                    }
                    else {
                        $(divpadre).height($(divpadre).attr('altezza'))
                        $(ul).height($(ul).attr('altezza'))
                    }



                    $('#detailsDialog').remove()


                    var div = $('<div id="detailsDialog"></div>')

                    var div2 = $('<div class="details-form-field"></div>');

                    var form = $('<form id="detailsForm"></form>')
                    var label = $("<label for='File'>File:</label>")
                    var file = $('<input id="File" class="inputDisabled" name="File" disabled="true" type="text" />');
                    div2.append(label);
                    div2.append(file);

                    form.append(div2);


                    var span = $('<span class="btn btn-success fileinput-button" style="width:60px;vertical-align:bottom;float:right"  ></span>');
                    var input = $('<input id="fileupload" type="file"  accept=".xlsx" name="files[]" multiple />');
                    var span2 = $('<span>+ Add file</span>')

                    span.append(input);
                    span.append(span2);
                    form.append(span);


                    var progress = $('<div id="progress" class="progress" style="display:none;width:230px"></div>')
                    progress.append($('<div class="progress-bar progress-bar-success"></div>'))
                    form.append(progress);


                    div.append(form);

                    divpadre.height(divpadre.height() + 130);
                    ul.height(ul.height() + 130);

                    $(sender).parent().append(div);


                    // aggiungo istruzioni x upload del file
                    $(function () {

                        $('#fileupload').fileupload({


                            url: urlFile,
                            //dataType: 'json',
                            add: function (e, data) {


                                UploadFileTitle = data.files[0].name;
                                UploadFileType = data.files[0].type;
                                $('#progress').show();
                                data.submit();
                            },
                            progress: function (e, data) {

                                // alert('Progress')

                                var progress = parseInt(data.loaded / data.total * 100, 10);
                                $('#progress .progress-bar').css(
                                    'width',
                                    progress + '%'
                                );

                            },
                            success: function (response, status) {

                                //	  alert('Success')
                                $('#progress').hide();
                                $('#progress .progress-bar').css('width', '0%');
                                UploadFileName = response;
                                $('#File').val(UploadFileTitle);
                                // ora devo forzare la compilazione
                            },
                            error: function (error) {
                                $('#progress').hide();
                                $('#progress .progress-bar').css('width', '0%');
                                //alert(error.statusText);
                                $('#erroriinnerPopup').html(error.responseText);
                                $('#errori').jqxWindow('open');
                            }
                        });
                    });

                    break;
            }
        }
